    10	export const useDashboardFilter = (): ComputedRef<FilterConfiguration> => {
    11	    const {t} = useI18n();
    12	
    13	    return computed(() => {
    14	        return {
    15	            title: t("filter.titles.dashboard_filters"),
    16	            searchPlaceholder: t("filter.search_placeholders.search_dashboards"),
    17	            keys: [
    18	                {
    19	                    key: "namespace",
    20	                    label: t("filter.namespace.label"),
    21	                    description: t("filter.namespace.description"),
    22	                    comparators: [
    23	                        Comparators.IN,
    24	                        Comparators.NOT_IN,
    25	                        Comparators.CONTAINS,
    26	                        Comparators.PREFIX,
    27	                    ],
    28	                    valueType: "multi-select",
    29	                    valueProvider: async () => {
    30	                        const user = useAuthStore().user;
    31	                        if (user && user.hasAnyActionOnAnyNamespace(permission.NAMESPACE, action.READ)) {
    32	                            const namespacesStore = useNamespacesStore();
    33	                            const namespaces = (await namespacesStore.loadAutocomplete()) as string[];
    34	                            return [...new Set(namespaces
    35	                                .flatMap(namespace => {
    36	                                    return namespace.split(".").reduce((current: string[], part: string) => {
    37	                                        const previousCombination = current?.[current.length - 1];
    38	                                        return [...current, `${(previousCombination ? previousCombination + "." : "")}${part}`];
    39	                                    }, []);
    40	                                }))].map(namespace => ({
    41	                                    label: namespace,
    42	                                    value: namespace
    43	                                }));
    44	                        }
    45	                        return [];
    46	                    },
    47	                    searchable: true
    48	                },
    49	                {
    50	                    key: "timeRange",
    51	                    label: t("filter.timeRange_dashboard.label"),
    52	                    description: t("filter.timeRange_dashboard.description"),
    53	                    comparators: [Comparators.EQUALS],
    54	                    valueType: "select",

     2	
     3	import {useRoute} from "vue-router";

     5	import {useDashboardStore} from "../../../stores/dashboard";
     6	
     7	import {useI18n} from "vue-i18n";
     8	
     9	import {decodeSearchParams} from "../../filter/utils/helpers";
    10	
    11	
    12	import {FilterObject} from "../../../utils/filters";
    13	import {Chart, Parameters, Request} from "../types.ts";
    14	
    15	
    16	
    17	export const isKPIChart = (type: string): boolean => type === "io.kestra.plugin.core.dashboard.chart.KPI";
    18	
    19	export const isTableChart = (type: string): boolean => type === "io.kestra.plugin.core.dashboard.chart.Table";
    20	
    21	export const getChartTitle = (chart: Chart): string => chart.chartOptions?.displayName ?? chart.id;
    22	
    23	export const getPropertyValue = (data: Record<string, any>, property: "value" | "description"): string => data.results?.[0]?.[property];
    24	
    25	export const isPaginationEnabled = (chart: Chart): boolean => chart.chartOptions?.pagination?.enabled ?? false;
    26	
    27	export const processFlowYaml = (yaml: string, namespace: string, flow: string): string => yaml.replace(/--NAMESPACE--/g, namespace).replace(/--FLOW--/g, flow);
    28	
    29	export const ALLOWED_CREATION_ROUTES = ["home", "flows/update", "namespaces/update"];
    30	
    31	export function useChartGenerator(dashboardId: string | undefined, props: {chart: Chart; filters: FilterObject[]; showDefault: boolean;}, includeHooks: boolean = true) {
    32	    const percentageShown = computed(() => props.chart?.chartOptions?.numberType === "PERCENTAGE");
    33	
    34	    const route = useRoute();
    35	
    36	    const dashboardStore = useDashboardStore();
    37	
    38	    const {t} = useI18n({useScope: "global"});
    39	    const EMPTY_TEXT = t("dashboards.empty");
    40	
    41	    const data = ref();
    42	    async function generate(pagination?: { pageNumber: number; pageSize: number }, customFilters?: FilterObject[]) {
    43	        const filters = customFilters ?? props.filters.concat(decodeSearchParams(route.query) ?? []);
    44	        const parameters: Parameters = {...pagination, filters: (filters ?? {})};
    45	
    46	        if (!props.showDefault) {
    47	            if(!dashboardId){
    48	                throw new Error("to generate charts from backend we need a dashboard id")
    49	            }
    50	            data.value = await dashboardStore.generate(dashboardId, props.chart.id, parameters);
    51	        } else {
    52	            if (!props.chart.content){
    53	                throw new Error("Chart content must exist for preview.");
    54	            }
    55	
    56	            const request: Request = {chart: props.chart.content, globalFilter: parameters};
    57	            data.value = await dashboardStore.chartPreview(request);
    58	        }
    59	
    60	        return data.value;
    61	    };
    62	
    63	    onMounted(async () => {
    64	        if (includeHooks) await generate();
    65	    });
    66	
    67	    return {percentageShown, EMPTY_TEXT, data, generate};
    68	}
    69	
    70	export * from "../types";

     2	import {AppliedFilter, Comparators} from "./filterTypes";
     3	
     4	const decodeURIComponentSafely = (value: string | (string | null)[]): string | string[] =>
     5	    Array.isArray(value)
     6	        ? value.filter(v => v !== null).map(decodeURIComponent)
     7	        : decodeURIComponent(value);
     8	
     9	export function getComparator(comparatorKey: keyof typeof Comparators): Comparators {
    10	    return Comparators[comparatorKey];
    11	}
    12	
    13	export function keyOfComparator(comparator: Comparators): keyof typeof Comparators {
    14	    return Object.entries(Comparators).find(([_, value]) => value === comparator)![0] as keyof typeof Comparators;
    15	}
    16	
    17	export const decodeSearchParams = (query: LocationQuery) =>
    18	    Object.entries(query)
    19	        .filter(([key]) => key.startsWith("filters[") || key === "q")
    20	        .map(([key, value]) => {
    21	            if (!value) return null;
    22	
    23	            const match = key.match(/filters\[(.*?)]\[(.*?)](?:\[(.*?)])?/);
    24	            if (!match) return null;
    25	
    26	            const [, field, operation, subKey] = match;
    27	
    28	            if (subKey) {
    29	                return {
    30	                    field,
    31	                    value: `${subKey}:${decodeURIComponentSafely(value)}`,
    32	                    operation
    33	                };
    34	            }
    35	
    36	            return {
    37	                field,
    38	                value: decodeURIComponentSafely(value),
    39	                operation
    40	            };
    41	        })
    42	        .filter(v => v !== null);
    43	
    44	type Filter = Pick<AppliedFilter, "key" | "comparator" | "value">;
    45	
    46	export const encodeFiltersToQuery = (filters: Filter[], keyOfComparator: (comparator: any) => string) =>
    47	    filters.reduce((query, filter) => {
    48	        const {key, comparator, value} = filter;
    49	        const comparatorKey = keyOfComparator(comparator);
    50	
    51	        switch (key) {
    52	            case "timeRange":
    53	                if (typeof value === "object" && "startDate" in value) {
    54	                    query["filters[startDate][GREATER_THAN_OR_EQUAL_TO]"] = value.startDate.toISOString();
    55	                    query["filters[endDate][LESS_THAN_OR_EQUAL_TO]"] = value.endDate.toISOString();
    56	                } else {
    57	                    query[`filters[${key}][${comparatorKey}]`] = value?.toString() ?? "";
    58	                }
    59	                return query;
    60	            default: {
    61	                if (Array.isArray(value) && value.some(v => typeof v === "string" && v.includes(":"))) {
    62	                    value.forEach((item: string) => {
    63	                        const [k, v] = item.split(":", 2);
    64	                        if (k && v) query[`filters[${key}][${comparatorKey}][${k}]`] = v;
    65	                    });
    66	                } else {
    67	                    query[`filters[${key}][${comparatorKey}]`] = Array.isArray(value)
    68	                        ? value.join(",")
    69	                        : value instanceof Date
    70	                            ? value.toISOString()
    71	                            : value?.toString() ?? "";
    72	                }
    73	                return query;
    74	            }
    75	        }
    76	    }, {} as Record<string, string>);
    77	
    78	export const isValidFilter = (filter: Filter): boolean => {
    79	    const {value} = filter;
    80	
    81	    if (value == null || value === "") return false;
    82	
    83	    switch (true) {
    84	        case Array.isArray(value):
    85	            return value.length > 0;
    86	        case typeof value === "object" && "startDate" in value:
    87	            return !!(value.startDate && value.endDate);
    88	        case value instanceof Date:
    89	            return true;
    90	        default:
    91	            return true;
    92	    }
    93	};
    94	
    95	export const getUniqueFilters = <T extends { key: string }>(filters: T[]): T[] =>
    96	    filters.filter((filter, index, self) =>
    97	        index === self.findLastIndex(f => f.key === filter.key)
    98	    );
    99	
   100	export const clearFilterQueryParams = (query: Record<string, any>): void => {
   101	    for (const key of Object.keys(query)) {
   102	        if (key.startsWith("filters[")) delete query[key];
   103	    }
   104	};
   105	
   106	export const isSearchPath = (name: string) =>
   107	    ["home", "flows/list", "executions/list", "logs/list", "admin/triggers"].includes(name);

   266	    @Post(uri = "{id}/charts/{chartId}")
   267	    @Operation(tags = { "Dashboards" }, summary = "Generate a dashboard chart data")
   268	    public PagedResults<Map<String, Object>> getDashboardChartData(
   269	        @Parameter(description = "The dashboard id") @PathVariable String id,
   270	        @Parameter(description = "The chart id") @PathVariable String chartId,
   271	        @RequestBody(description = "The filters to apply, some can override chart definition like labels & namespace") @Body ChartFiltersOverrides globalFilter) throws IOException {
   272	        var fetchChartDataQuery = buildDashboardChardDataQuery(id, chartId, globalFilter);
   273	
   274	        if (fetchChartDataQuery == null)
   275	            return null;
   276	
   277	        return fetchChartData(fetchChartDataQuery);
   278	    }
   279	
   280	    private FetchChartDataQuery buildDashboardChardDataQuery(String id, String chartId, ChartFiltersOverrides globalFilter) {
   281	        String tenantId = tenantService.resolveTenant();
   282	        List<QueryFilter> filters = globalFilter.getFilters();
   283	
   284	        filters = formatLabelsFilters(filters);
   285	
   286	        Dashboard dashboard = dashboardRepository.get(tenantId, id).orElse(null);
   287	        if (dashboard == null) {
   288	            return null;
   289	        }
   290	
   291	        TimeLineSearch timeLineSearch = TimeLineSearch.extractFrom(filters);
   292	        validateTimeline(timeLineSearch.getStartDate(), timeLineSearch.getEndDate());
   293	
   294	        ZonedDateTime endDate = timeLineSearch.getEndDate();
   295	        ZonedDateTime startDate = timeLineSearch.getStartDate();
   296	
   297	        if (startDate == null) {
   298	            // If no start date is provided, we use the default duration of the dashboard's time
   299	            startDate = endDate.minus(dashboard.getTimeWindow().getDefaultDuration());
   300	        }
   301	
   302	        if (endDate != null && endDate.isBefore(startDate)) {
   303	            throw new IllegalArgumentException("`endDate` must be after `startDate`.");
   304	        }
   305	
   306	        Duration windowDuration = Duration.ofSeconds((endDate != null ? endDate : ZonedDateTime.now()).minus(Duration.ofSeconds(startDate.toEpochSecond())).toEpochSecond());
   307	        if (windowDuration.compareTo(dashboard.getTimeWindow().getMax()) > 0) {
   308	            throw new IllegalArgumentException("The queried window is larger than the max allowed one.");
   309	        }
   310	
   311	        Chart<?> chart = dashboard.getCharts().stream().filter(g -> g.getId().equals(chartId)).findFirst().orElse(null);
   312	        if (chart == null) {
   313	            return null;
   314	        }
   315	        var pageNumber = globalFilter.getPageNumber();
   316	        var pageSize = globalFilter.getPageSize();
   317	        var pageable = pageNumber != null && pageSize != null ? PageableUtils.from(pageNumber, pageSize) : null;
   318	
   319	        return new FetchChartDataQuery(chart, filters, startDate, endDate, tenantId, pageable);
   320	    }
   321	
   322	    private List<QueryFilter> formatLabelsFilters(List<QueryFilter> filters) {
   323	        return Optional.ofNullable(filters)
   324	            .map(queryFilters -> queryFilters.stream().map(f ->
   325	            {
   326	                if (f.field() == QueryFilter.Field.LABELS && f.value() instanceof String filterStr) {
   327	                    return QueryFilter.builder()
   328	                        .field(f.field())
   329	                        .operation(f.operation())
   330	                        .value(Label.from(filterStr))
   331	                        .build();
   332	                }
   333	                return f;
   334	            }).toList())
   335	            .orElse(null);
   336	    }

   341	    public PagedResults<Map<String, Object>> previewChart(
   342	        @Parameter(description = "The chart") @Body @Valid PreviewRequest previewRequest) throws IOException {
   343	        var fetchChartDataQuery = buildChartPreviewDataQuery(previewRequest);
   344	        return fetchChartData(fetchChartDataQuery);
   345	    }
   346	
   347	    private FetchChartDataQuery buildChartPreviewDataQuery(PreviewRequest previewRequest) {
   348	        String tenantId = tenantService.resolveTenant();
   349	        Chart<?> chart = YamlParser.parse(previewRequest.chart(), Chart.class);
   350	        ChartFiltersOverrides globalFilter = previewRequest.globalFilter();
   351	
   352	        List<QueryFilter> filters = globalFilter != null ? globalFilter.getFilters() : null;
   353	
   354	        filters = formatLabelsFilters(filters);
   355	
   356	        ZonedDateTime endDate = null;
   357	        ZonedDateTime startDate;
   358	        if (filters != null) {
   359	            TimeLineSearch timeLineSearch = TimeLineSearch.extractFrom(filters);
   360	            validateTimeline(timeLineSearch.getStartDate(), timeLineSearch.getEndDate());
   361	
   362	            endDate = timeLineSearch.getEndDate();
   363	            startDate = timeLineSearch.getStartDate();
   364	        } else {
   365	            startDate = ZonedDateTime.now().minusDays(8);
   366	        }
   367	
   368	        if (endDate != null && endDate.isBefore(startDate)) {
   369	            throw new IllegalArgumentException("`endDate` must be after `startDate`.");
   370	        }
   371	        Pageable pageable = null;
   372	        if (globalFilter != null && globalFilter.getPageSize() != null && globalFilter.getPageNumber() != null) {
   373	            pageable = PageableUtils.from(globalFilter.getPageNumber(), globalFilter.getPageSize());
   374	        }
   375	
   376	        return new FetchChartDataQuery(chart, filters, startDate, endDate, tenantId, pageable);
   377	    }
   378	
   379	    private record FetchChartDataQuery(Chart<?> chart, List<QueryFilter> filters, ZonedDateTime startDate,
   380	        ZonedDateTime endDate, String tenantId, Pageable pageable) {
   381	    }
   382	
   383	    @SuppressWarnings({ "rawtypes", "unchecked" })
   384	    private PagedResults<Map<String, Object>> fetchChartData(FetchChartDataQuery fetchChartDataQuery) throws IOException {
   385	        var chart = fetchChartDataQuery.chart();
   386	        var filters = fetchChartDataQuery.filters();
   387	        var startDate = fetchChartDataQuery.startDate();
   388	        var endDate = fetchChartDataQuery.endDate();
   389	        var tenantId = fetchChartDataQuery.tenantId();
   390	        var pageable = fetchChartDataQuery.pageable();
   391	
   392	        if (chart instanceof DataChart dataChart) {
   393	            DataFilter<?, ?> dataChartDatas = dataChart.getData();
   394	            dataChartDatas.updateWhereWithGlobalFilters(filters, startDate, endDate);
   395	
   396	            // StartDate & EndDate are only set in the globalFilter for JDBC
   397	            // TODO: Check if we can remove them from generate() for ElasticSearch as they are already set in the where property
   398	            return PagedResults.of(this.dashboardRepository.generate(tenantId, dataChart, startDate, endDate, pageable));
   399	        } else if (chart instanceof DataChartKPI dataChartKPI) {
   400	            DataFilterKPI<?, ?> dataChartDatas = dataChartKPI.getData();
   401	            dataChartDatas.updateWhereWithGlobalFilters(filters, startDate, endDate);
   402	
   403	            return PagedResults.of(new ArrayListTotal<>(this.dashboardRepository.generateKPI(tenantId, dataChartKPI, startDate, endDate), 1));
   404	        } else if (chart instanceof Markdown markdownChart) {
   405	            if (markdownChart.getSource() != null && markdownChart.getSource() instanceof FlowDescription flowDescription) {
   406	                Optional<Flow> optionalFlow = flowRepository.findById(tenantId, flowDescription.getNamespace(), flowDescription.getFlowId());
   407	                if (optionalFlow.isPresent()) {
   408	                    Flow flow = optionalFlow.get();
   409	                    Map<String, Object> descriptionMap = Map.of(
   410	                        "description", flow.getDescription() != null ? flow.getDescription() : ""

    17	        List<AbstractFilter<Fields>> updatedWhere = where != null ? new ArrayList<>(where) : new ArrayList<>();
    18	
    19	        if (filters != null) {
    20	            List<QueryFilter> namespaceFilters = filters.stream().filter(f -> f.field().equals(QueryFilter.Field.NAMESPACE)).toList();

    22	                updatedWhere.removeIf(filter -> filter.getField().equals(Fields.NAMESPACE));

    25	                    updatedWhere.add(f.toDashboardFilterBuilder(Fields.NAMESPACE, f.value()));
    26	                });
    27	            }

    36	                    } else {
    37	                        updatedWhere.add(Contains.<Fields> builder().field(Fields.LABELS).value(f.value()).build());
    38	                    }
    39	                });
    40	            }
    41

    44	                updatedWhere.removeIf(filter -> filter.getField().equals(Fields.FLOW_ID));

    48	                });
    49	            }

    57	                });

    33	        this.value = value;
    34	    }
    35	
    36	    public enum Op {
    37	        EQUALS,
    38	        NOT_EQUALS,
    39	        GREATER_THAN,
    40	        LESS_THAN,
    41	        GREATER_THAN_OR_EQUAL_TO,
    42	        LESS_THAN_OR_EQUAL_TO,
    43	        IN,
    44	        NOT_IN,
    45	        STARTS_WITH,
    46	        ENDS_WITH,
    47	        CONTAINS,
    48	        REGEX,
    49	        PREFIX
    50	    }
    51	
    52	    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
    53	    private List<Object> asValues(Object value) {
    54	        if (value instanceof String valueStr) {
    55	            Object[] parts = valueStr.split(",");
    56	            return Arrays.asList(parts);
    57	        }
    58	        return (List<Object>) value;
    59	    }
    60	
    61	    public <T extends Enum<T>> AbstractFilter<T> toDashboardFilterBuilder(T field, Object value) {
    62	        return switch (this.operation) {
    63	            case EQUALS -> EqualTo.<T> builder().field(field).value(value).build();
    64	            case NOT_EQUALS -> NotEqualTo.<T> builder().field(field).value(value).build();
    65	            case GREATER_THAN -> GreaterThan.<T> builder().field(field).value(value).build();
    66	            case LESS_THAN -> LessThan.<T> builder().field(field).value(value).build();
    67	            case GREATER_THAN_OR_EQUAL_TO -> GreaterThanOrEqualTo.<T> builder().field(field).value(value).build();
    68	            case LESS_THAN_OR_EQUAL_TO -> LessThanOrEqualTo.<T> builder().field(field).value(value).build();
    69	            case IN -> In.<T> builder().field(field).values(asValues(value)).build();
    70	            case NOT_IN -> NotIn.<T> builder().field(field).values(asValues(value)).build();
    71	            case STARTS_WITH -> StartsWith.<T> builder().field(field).value(value.toString()).build();
    72	            case ENDS_WITH -> EndsWith.<T> builder().field(field).value(value.toString()).build();
    73	            case CONTAINS -> Contains.<T> builder().field(field).value(value.toString()).build();
    74	            case REGEX -> Regex.<T> builder().field(field).value(value.toString()).build();
    75	            case PREFIX -> Prefix.<T> builder().field(field).value(value.toString()).build();
    76	        };
    77	    }

   520	    private Condition applyDateCondition(OffsetDateTime dateTime, QueryFilter.Op operation, String fieldName) {
   521	        return switch (operation) {
   522	            case LESS_THAN -> field(fieldName).lessThan(dateTime);
   523	            case LESS_THAN_OR_EQUAL_TO -> field(fieldName).lessOrEqual(dateTime);
   524	            case GREATER_THAN -> field(fieldName).greaterThan(dateTime);
   525	            case GREATER_THAN_OR_EQUAL_TO -> field(fieldName).greaterOrEqual(dateTime);
   526	            case EQUALS -> field(fieldName).eq(dateTime);
   527	            case NOT_EQUALS -> field(fieldName).ne(dateTime);
   528	            default ->
   529	                throw new InvalidQueryFiltersException("Unsupported operation for date condition: " + operation);
   530	        };
   531	    }

   533	    private Condition applyScopeCondition(Object value, QueryFilter.Op operation) {
   534	        List<FlowScope> flowScopes = Enums.fromList(value, FlowScope.class);
   535	        if (flowScopes.size() > 1) {
   536	            throw new InvalidQueryFiltersException("Only one scope can be use in the same time");
   537	        }
   538	        FlowScope scope = flowScopes.getFirst();
   539	
   540	        String systemNamespace = this.kestraConfig.getSystemFlowNamespace();
   541	        return switch (operation) {
   542	            case EQUALS -> FlowScope.USER.equals(scope) ? field("namespace").ne(systemNamespace) : field("namespace").eq(systemNamespace);
   543	            case NOT_EQUALS -> FlowScope.USER.equals(scope) ? field("namespace").eq(systemNamespace) : field("namespace").ne(systemNamespace);
   544	            default -> throw new InvalidQueryFiltersException("Unsupported operation for SCOPE: " + operation);
   545	        };
   546	    }

   413	    }

   416	        throw new InvalidQueryFiltersException("Unsupported operation: " + operation);
   417	    }
   418	
   419	    protected Condition findMetadataCondition(Map<?, ?> metadata, QueryFilter.Op operation) {
   420	        throw new InvalidQueryFiltersException("Unsupported operation: " + operation);
   421	    }
   422	
   423	    protected Condition getEnabledCondition(Object value, Op operation) {
   424	        return defaultHandlers(QueryFilter.Field.ENABLED, value, operation);
   425	    }
   426	
   427	    // Generate the condition for Field.STATE
   428	    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
   429	    protected Condition generateStateCondition(Object value, QueryFilter.Op operation) {
   430	        List<State.Type> stateList = switch (value) {
   431	            case List<?> list when !list.isEmpty() && list.getFirst() instanceof State.Type -> (List<State.Type>) list;
   432	            case List<?> list -> list.stream().map(item -> State.Type.valueOf(item.toString())).toList();
   433	            case State.Type state -> List.of(state);
   434	            case String state -> List.of(State.Type.valueOf(state));
   435	            default ->
   436	                throw new InvalidQueryFiltersException("Field 'state' requires a State.Type or List<State.Type> value");
   437	        };
   438	
   439	        return switch (operation) {
   440	            case IN, EQUALS -> statesFilter(stateList);
   441	            case NOT_IN, NOT_EQUALS -> DSL.not(statesFilter(stateList));
   442	            default -> throw new InvalidQueryFiltersException("Unsupported operation for State.Type: " + operation);
   443	        };
   444	    }
   445	
   446	    protected Condition statusCondition(Object value, QueryFilter.Op operation) {
   447	        return defaultHandlers(QueryFilter.Field.STATUS, value, operation);
   448	    }

   451	        throw new InvalidQueryFiltersException("Unsupported operation: " + operation);

    72	    import {computed, ref} from "vue";

    77	    const props = defineProps<{
    78	        label?: string;
    79	        filterKey?: string;
    80	        modelValue: string[];
    81	        searchable?: boolean;
    82	        placeholder?: string;
    83	        options: {value: string; label: string}[];
    84	    }>();
    85	
    86	    const emits = defineEmits<{
    87	        "apply": [];
    88	        "reset": [];
    89	        "update:modelValue": [value: string[]];
    90	    }>();
    91	
    92	    const searchQuery = ref("");
    93	
    94	    const filteredOptions = computed(() => {
    95	        const query = searchQuery.value.trim().toLowerCase();
    96	        return query
    97	            ? props.options.filter(option =>
    98	                option.label.toLowerCase().includes(query) ||
    99	                option.value.toLowerCase().includes(query)
   100	            )
   101	            : props.options;
   102	    });
   103	
   104	    const allSelected = computed(
   105	        () =>
   106	            filteredOptions.value.length > 0 &&
   107	            filteredOptions.value.every(option => props.modelValue.includes(option.value))
   108	    );
   109	
   110	    const isPartiallySelected = computed(() => {
   111	        const options = filteredOptions.value;
   112	        if (!options.length) return false;
   113	        const selectedCount = options.filter(opt => props.modelValue.includes(opt.value)).length;
   114	        return selectedCount > 0 && selectedCount < options.length;
   115	    });
   116	
   117	    const handleSelectAllChange = (checked: boolean) => {
   118	        const values = new Set(props.modelValue);
   119	        filteredOptions.value.forEach(opt =>
   120	            checked ? values.add(opt.value) : values.delete(opt.value)
   121	        );
   122	        emits("update:modelValue", [...values]);
   123	    };
   124	
   125	    const handleDeselectAllChange = (checked: boolean) => {
   126	        if (checked) {
   127	            const values = new Set(props.modelValue);
   128	            filteredOptions.value.forEach(opt => values.delete(opt.value));
   129	            emits("update:modelValue", [...values]);
   130	        }
   131	    };
   132	
   133	    const handleOptionChange = (value: string, checked: boolean) =>
   134	        emits(
   135	            "update:modelValue",
   136	            checked ? [...props.modelValue, value] : props.modelValue.filter(v => v !== value)
   137	        );
   138	</script>

    31	
    32	        return switch (agg) {
    33	            case AVG -> avg(field.cast(Double.class));
    34	            case MAX -> max(field.cast(Double.class));
    35	            case MIN -> min(field.cast(Double.class));
    36	            case SUM -> sum(field.cast(Double.class));

   614	    public static void validateQueryFilters(List<QueryFilter> filters, Resource resource) {
   615	        if (filters == null) {
   616	            return;
   617	        }
   618	        List<String> errors = new ArrayList<>();
   619	        filters.forEach(filter ->
   620	        {
   621	            if (!filter.field().supportedOp().contains(filter.operation())) {
   622	                errors.add(
   623	                    "Operation %s is not supported for field %s. Supported operations are %s".formatted(
   624	                        filter.operation(), filter.field().name(),
   625	                        filter.field().supportedOp().stream().map(Op::name).collect(Collectors.joining(", "))
   626	                    )
   627	                );
   628	            }
   629	            if (!resource.supportedField().contains(filter.field())) {
   630	                errors.add(
   631	                    "Field %s is not supported for resource %s. Supported fields are %s".formatted(
   632	                        filter.field().name(), resource.name(),
   633	                        resource.supportedField().stream().map(Field::name).collect(Collectors.joining(", "))
   634	                    )
   635	                );
   636	            }
   637	        });
   638	        if (!errors.isEmpty()) {
   639	            throw new InvalidQueryFiltersException(errors);
   640	        }
   641	    }

    25	            {
    26	                updatedWhere.add(EqualTo.<ITriggers.Fields> builder().field(ITriggers.Fields.NAMESPACE).value(f.value()).build());
    27	            });
    28	        }
    29	
    30	        List<QueryFilter> flowFilters = filters.stream().filter(f -> f.field().equals(QueryFilter.Field.FLOW_ID)).toList();
    31	        if (!flowFilters.isEmpty()) {
    32	            updatedWhere.removeIf(filter -> filter.getField().equals(Fields.FLOW_ID));
    33	            flowFilters.forEach(f ->
    34	            {
    35	                updatedWhere.add(f.toDashboardFilterBuilder(Fields.FLOW_ID, f.value()));
    36	            });
    37	        }
    38	
    39	        return updatedWhere;
    40	    }
    41	
    42	    enum Fields {
    43	        ID,
    44	        NAMESPACE,
    45	        FLOW_ID,
    46	        TRIGGER_ID,
    47	        EXECUTION_ID,
    48	        NEXT_EXECUTION_DATE,
    49	        WORKER_ID
    50	    }
    51	}
    52

     2	import {useRoute, useRouter} from "vue-router";
     3	import {
     4	    keyOfComparator,
     5	    decodeSearchParams,
     6	    encodeFiltersToQuery,
     7	    isValidFilter,
     8	    getUniqueFilters,
     9	    clearFilterQueryParams
    10	} from "../utils/helpers";
    11	import {
    12	    AppliedFilter,
    13	    FilterConfiguration,
    14	    FilterKeyConfig,
    15	    COMPARATOR_LABELS,
    16	    Comparators,
    17	    TEXT_COMPARATORS,
    18	} from "../utils/filterTypes";
    19	import {usePreAppliedFilters} from "./usePreAppliedFilters";
    20	import {applyDefaultFilters, useDefaultFilter} from "./useDefaultFilter";
    21	
    22	export function useFilters(
    23	    configuration: FilterConfiguration,
    24	    showSearchInput = true,
    25	    defaultScope?: boolean,
    26	    defaultTimeRange?: boolean,
    27	    defaultDuration?: string,
    28	) {
    29	    const router = useRouter();
    30	    const route = useRoute();
    31	
    32	    const appliedFilters = ref<AppliedFilter[]>([]);
    33	    const searchQuery = ref("");
    34	    const dismissedDefaultVisibleKeys = ref<Set<string>>(new Set());
    35	
    36	    const {
    37	        markAsPreApplied,
    38	        hasPreApplied,
    39	        getPreApplied
    40	    } = usePreAppliedFilters();
    41	
    42	    const isDefaultVisibleKey = (key: string) =>
    43	        configuration.keys?.some((k) => k.key === key && k.visibleByDefault) ?? false;
    44	
    45	    const dismissDefaultVisibleKey = (key: string) => {
    46	        if (!isDefaultVisibleKey(key)) {
    47	            return;
    48	        }
    49	
    50	        const next = new Set(dismissedDefaultVisibleKeys.value);
    51	        next.add(key);
    52	        dismissedDefaultVisibleKeys.value = next;
    53	    };
    54	
    55	    const restoreDefaultVisibleKey = (key: string) => {
    56	        if (!dismissedDefaultVisibleKeys.value.has(key)) {
    57	            return;
    58	        }
    59	
    60	        const next = new Set(dismissedDefaultVisibleKeys.value);
    61	        next.delete(key);
    62	        dismissedDefaultVisibleKeys.value = next;
    63	    };
    64	
    65	    const dismissAllDefaultVisibleKeys = () => {
    66	        dismissedDefaultVisibleKeys.value = new Set(
    67	            configuration.keys
    68	                ?.filter((key) => key.visibleByDefault)
    69	                .map((key) => key.key) ?? []
    70	        );
    71	    };
    72	
    73	    const resetDismissedDefaultVisibleKeys = () => {
    74	        dismissedDefaultVisibleKeys.value = new Set();
    75	    };
    76	
    77	    const hasDismissedDefaultVisibleKeys = computed(
    78	        () => dismissedDefaultVisibleKeys.value.size > 0
    79	    );
    80	
    81	    const updateSearchQuery = (query: Record<string, any>) => {
    82	        const trimmedQuery = searchQuery.value?.trim();
    83	        delete query.q;
    84	        delete query.search;
    85	        delete query["filters[q][EQUALS]"];
    86	
    87	        if (trimmedQuery && showSearchInput) {
    88	            query["filters[q][EQUALS]"] = trimmedQuery;
    89	        }
    90	    };
    91	
    92	    const hasValue = (filter: AppliedFilter): boolean => {
    93	        return (Array.isArray(filter.value) && filter.value.length > 0) ||
    94	            (!Array.isArray(filter.value) && filter.value !== "" && filter.value !== null && filter.value !== undefined);
    95	    };
    96	
    97	    const updateRoute = (shouldResetPage = false) => {
    98	        const query = {...route.query};
    99	        clearFilterQueryParams(query);
   100	
   101	        Object.assign(query, encodeFiltersToQuery(getUniqueFilters(appliedFilters.value
   102	            .filter(isValidFilter)), keyOfComparator));
   103	
   104	        updateSearchQuery(query);
   105	
   106	        if (shouldResetPage && parseInt(String(query.page ?? "1")) > 1) {
   107	            delete query.page;
   108	        }
   109	
   110	        router.push({query});
   111	    };
   112	
   113	    const createAppliedFilter = (
   114	        key: string,
   115	        config: any,
   116	        comparator: Comparators,
   117	        value: any,
   118	        valueLabel: string,
   119	        idSuffix: string
   120	    ): AppliedFilter => ({
   121	        id: `${key}-${idSuffix}-${Date.now()}`,
   122	        key,
   123	        keyLabel: config?.label,
   124	        comparator,
   125	        comparatorLabel: COMPARATOR_LABELS[comparator],
   126	        value,
   127	        valueLabel
   128	    });
   129	
   130	    const createTimeRangeFilter = (
   131	        config: any,
   132	        startDate: Date,
   133	        endDate: Date,
   134	        comparator = Comparators.EQUALS
   135	    ): AppliedFilter => {
   136	        return {
   137	            ...createAppliedFilter(
   138	                "timeRange",
   139	                config,
   140	                comparator,
   141	                {startDate, endDate},
   142	                `${startDate.toLocaleDateString()} - ${endDate.toLocaleDateString()}`,
   143	                keyOfComparator(comparator)
   144	            ),
   145	            comparatorLabel: "Is Between"
   146	        };
   147	    };
   148	
   149	    const processFieldValue = (config: any, params: any[], _field: string, comparator: Comparators) => {
   150	        const isTextOp = TEXT_COMPARATORS.includes(comparator);
   151	
   152	        if (config?.valueType === "key-value") {
   153	            const combinedValue = params.map(p => p?.value as string);
   154	            return {
   155	                value: combinedValue,
   156	                valueLabel: combinedValue.length > 1
   157	                    ? `${combinedValue[0]} +${combinedValue.length - 1}`
   158	                    : combinedValue[0] ?? ""
   159	            };
   160	        }
   161	
   162	        if (config?.valueType === "multi-select" && !isTextOp) {
   163	            const combinedValue = params.flatMap(p =>
   164	                Array.isArray(p?.value) ? p.value : (p?.value as string)?.split(",") ?? []
   165	            );
   166	            return {
   167	                value: combinedValue,
   168	                valueLabel: combinedValue.join(", ")
   169	            };
   170	        }
   171	
   172	        let value = Array.isArray(params[0]?.value)
   173	            ? params[0].value[0]
   174	            : (params[0]?.value as string);
   175	
   176	        if (config?.valueType === "date" && typeof value === "string") {
   177	            value = new Date(value);
   178	        }
   179	
   180	        return {
   181	            value,
   182	            valueLabel: value instanceof Date ? value.toLocaleDateString() : value
   183	        };
   184	    };
   185	
   186	    const parseEncodedFilters = (): AppliedFilter[] => {
   187	        const filtersMap = new Map<string, AppliedFilter>();
   188	        const dateFilters: Record<string, {comparatorKey: string; value: string}> = {};
   189	        const fieldParams = new Map<string, any[]>();
   190	
   191	        decodeSearchParams(route.query).forEach(param => {
   192	            if (!param) return;
   193	            if (["startDate", "endDate"].includes(param?.field)) {
   194	                dateFilters[param.field] = {
   195	                    comparatorKey: param?.operation ?? "",
   196	                    value: param?.value as string
   197	                };
   198	            } else {
   199	                if (!fieldParams.has(param?.field)) fieldParams.set(param.field, []);
   200	                fieldParams.get(param?.field)!.push(param);
   201	            }
   202	        });
   203	
   204	        fieldParams.forEach((params, field) => {
   205	            const config = configuration.keys?.find(k => k?.key === field);
   206	            if (!config) return;
   207	
   208	            const parsedComparator = Comparators[params[0]?.operation as keyof typeof Comparators];
   209	            const comparator = config.comparators?.includes(parsedComparator)
   210	                ? parsedComparator
   211	                : undefined;
   212	            if (!comparator) return;
   213	
   214	            const {value, valueLabel} = processFieldValue(config, params, field, comparator);
   215	            filtersMap.set(
   216	                field,
   217	                createAppliedFilter(field, config, comparator, value, valueLabel, params[0]?.operation)
   218	            );
   219	        });
   220	
   221	        if (dateFilters.startDate && dateFilters.endDate) {
   222	            const timeRangeConfig = configuration.keys?.find(k => k?.key === "timeRange");
   223	            if (timeRangeConfig) {
   224	                const comparator = Comparators[
   225	                    dateFilters.startDate?.comparatorKey as keyof typeof Comparators
   226	                ];
   227	                filtersMap.set(
   228	                    "timeRange",
   229	                    createTimeRangeFilter(
   230	                        timeRangeConfig,
   231	                        new Date(dateFilters.startDate?.value),
   232	                        new Date(dateFilters.endDate?.value),
   233	                        comparator
   234	                    )
   235	                );
   236	            }
   237	        }
   238	
   239	        return Array.from(filtersMap.values());
   240	    };
   241	
   242	        /**
   243	        * Initialize default visible filters. These filters are marked with visibleByDefault: true
   244	        * and are automatically added to the filter list when the page loads, even if no value
   245	        * are present to filter. Users can remove them, but they will reappear on page refresh.
   246	        */
   247	
   248	    const resolveDefaultVisibleValue = (key: FilterKeyConfig): AppliedFilter["value"] => {
   249	        const value = typeof key.defaultValue === "function"
   250	            ? key.defaultValue()
   251	            : key.defaultValue;
   252	
   253	        if (value !== undefined) {
   254	            return value;
   255	        }
   256	
   257	        return key.valueType === "multi-select" ? [] : "";
   258	    };
   259	
   260	    const defaultVisibleValueLabel = (value: AppliedFilter["value"]) => {

     8	    includeTimeRange?: boolean;
     9	    includeScope?: boolean;
    10	    /**
    11	     * Duration from dashboard's timeWindow.default (e.g. "P7D").
    12	     * Falls back to chartDefaultDuration from config endpoint -> then "PT24H".
    13	    **/
    14	    defaultDuration?: string;
    15	}
    16	
    17	const NAMESPACE_FILTER_PREFIX = "filters[namespace]";
    18	const SCOPE_FILTER_PREFIX = "filters[scope]";
    19	const TIME_RANGE_FILTER_PREFIX = "filters[timeRange]";
    20	
    21	const hasFilterKey = (query: LocationQuery, prefix: string): boolean =>
    22	    Object.keys(query).some(key => key.startsWith(prefix));
    23	
    24	export function applyDefaultFilters(
    25	    currentQuery?: LocationQuery,
    26	    {
    27	        namespace,
    28	        includeTimeRange,
    29	        includeScope,
    30	        defaultDuration,
    31	    }: DefaultFilterOptions = {}): { query: LocationQuery, change: boolean } {
    32	
    33	    const query = {...currentQuery};
    34	    let change = false;
    35	
    36	    if (namespace !== null && defaultNamespace() && !hasFilterKey(query, NAMESPACE_FILTER_PREFIX)) {
    37	        query[`${NAMESPACE_FILTER_PREFIX}[PREFIX]`] = defaultNamespace();
    38	        change = true;
    39	    }
    40	
    41	    if (includeScope && !hasFilterKey(query, SCOPE_FILTER_PREFIX)) {
    42	        query[`${SCOPE_FILTER_PREFIX}[EQUALS]`] = "USER";
    43	        change = true;
    44	    }
    45	
    46	    const TIME_FILTER_KEYS = /startDate|endDate|timeRange/;
    47	
    48	    if (includeTimeRange) {
    49	        const hasExisting = Object.keys(query).some(key => TIME_FILTER_KEYS.test(key));
    50	        if (!hasExisting || defaultDuration) {
    51	            if (hasExisting) {
    52	                Object.keys(query).forEach(key => { if (TIME_FILTER_KEYS.test(key)) delete query[key]; });
    53	            }
    54	            const duration = defaultDuration ?? useMiscStore().configs?.chartDefaultDuration ?? "PT24H";
    55	            query[`${TIME_RANGE_FILTER_PREFIX}[EQUALS]`] = duration;
    56	            change = true;
    57	        }
    58	    }
    59	
    60	    if (!includeScope) {
    61	        Object.keys(query).forEach(key => {
    62	            if (key.startsWith(SCOPE_FILTER_PREFIX)) {
    63	                delete query[key];
    64	                change = true;
    65	            }
    66	        });
    67	    }
    68	
    69	    return {query, change};
    70	}
    71	
    72	export function useDefaultFilter(
    73	    defaultOptions?: DefaultFilterOptions,
    74	) {
    75	    const route = useRoute();
    76	    const router = useRouter();
    77	
    78	    onMounted(async () => {
    79	        // wait for router to be ready
    80	        await nextTick()
    81	        // wait for the useRestoreUrl to apply its changes
    82	        await nextTick()
    83	        // finally add default filter if necessary
    84	        const {query, change} = applyDefaultFilters(route.query, defaultOptions)
    85	        if(change) {
    86	            router.replace({...route, query})
    87	        }
    88	    });
    89	
    90	    function resetDefaultFilter(){
    91	        router.replace({
    92	            ...route,
    93	            query: applyDefaultFilters({}, defaultOptions).query
    94	        });
    95	    }
    96	
    97	    return {
    98	        resetDefaultFilter
    99	    }
   100	}

/testbed/core/src/main/java/io/kestra/core/utils/Enums.java:19:public final class Enums {
package io.kestra.core.utils;

import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.function.Predicate;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;
import java.util.stream.Collectors;

import jakarta.annotation.Nullable;
import jakarta.validation.constraints.NotNull;

/**
 * Utility method for Enums.
 */
public final class Enums {

    public static final Pattern NORMALIZE = Pattern.compile("([a-z])([A-Z])");

    /**
     * Gets the enum for specified string name.
     *
     * @param value The enum raw value.
     * @param enumType The enum class type.
     * @param <T> The enum type.
     * @return The Enum.
     * @throws IllegalArgumentException if no enum exists for the specified value.
     */
    public static <T extends Enum<T>> T getForNameIgnoreCase(final @Nullable String value,
        final @NotNull Class<T> enumType,
        final T defaultValue) {
        if (value == null)
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported value 'null'");

        T[] values = enumType.getEnumConstants();
        return Arrays.stream(values)
            .filter(e -> e.name().equals(value.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT)))
            .findFirst()
            .orElse(defaultValue);
    }

    /**
     * Gets the enum for specified string name.
     *
     * @param value The enum raw value.
     * @param enumType The enum class type.
     * @param <T> The enum type.
     * @return The Enum.
     * @throws IllegalArgumentException if no enum exists for the specified value.
     */
    public static <T extends Enum<T>> T getForNameIgnoreCase(final @Nullable String value,
        final @NotNull Class<T> enumType) {
        return getForNameIgnoreCase(value, enumType, Map.of());

    }

    /**
     * Gets the enum for specified string name.
     *
     * @param value The enum raw value.
     * @param enumType The enum class type.
     * @param fallback The fallback map for unknown string.
     * @param <T> The enum type.
     * @return The Enum.
     * @throws IllegalArgumentException if no enum exists for the specified value.
     */
    public static <T extends Enum<T>> T getForNameIgnoreCase(final @Nullable String value,
        final @NotNull Class<T> enumType,
        final @NotNull Map<String, T> fallback) {
        if (value == null)
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported value 'null'");

        final Map<String, T> fallbackMap = fallback.entrySet()
            .stream()
            .collect(Collectors.toMap(entry -> entry.getKey().toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT), Map.Entry::getValue));

        T[] values = enumType.getEnumConstants();
        return Arrays.stream(values)
            .filter(e -> e.name().equals(value.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT)))
            .findFirst()
            .or(() -> Optional.ofNullable(fallbackMap.get(value.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT))))
            .orElseThrow(
                () -> new IllegalArgumentException(
                    String.format(
                        "Unsupported enum value '%s'. Expected one of: %s",
                        value,
                        Arrays.stream(values)
                            .map(Enum::name)
                            .collect(Collectors.joining(", ", "[", "]"))
                    )
                )
            );
    }

    /**
     * Gets all the enum values except the one to exclude.
     *
     * @param enumType The enum class type.
     * @param toExclude The enum values to exclude.
     * @param <T> The enum type.
     * @return The Enum value.
     */
    public static <T extends Enum<T>> Set<T> allExcept(final @NotNull Class<T> enumType, Set<T> toExclude) {
        T[] values = enumType.getEnumConstants();
        return Arrays.stream(values)
            .filter(Predicate.not(toExclude::contains))
            .collect(Collectors.toSet());
    }

    /**
     * Converts a string to its corresponding enum value based on a provided mapping.
     *
     * @param value The string representation of the enum value.
     * @param mapping A map of string values to enum constants.
     * @param typeName A descriptive name of the enum type (used in error messages).
     * @param <T> The type of the enum.
     * @return The corresponding enum constant.
     * @throws IllegalArgumentException If the string does not match any enum value.
     */
    public static <T extends Enum<T>> T fromString(String value, Map<String, T> mapping, String typeName) {
        return Optional.ofNullable(mapping.get(value))
            .orElseThrow(
                () -> new IllegalArgumentException(
                    "Unsupported %s '%s'. Expected one of: %s".formatted(typeName, value, mapping.keySet())
                )
            );
    }

    /**
     * Convert an object to a list of a specific enum.
     * 
     * @param value the object to convert to list of enum.
     * @param enumClass the class of the enum to convert to.
     * @return A list of the corresponding enum type
     * @param <T> The type of the enum.
     * @throws IllegalArgumentException If the value does not match any enum value.
     */
    public static <T extends Enum<T>> List<T> fromList(Object value, Class<T> enumClass) {
        return switch (value) {
            case List<?> list when !list.isEmpty() && enumClass.isInstance(list.getFirst()) -> (List<T>) list;
            case List<?> list when !list.isEmpty() && list.getFirst() instanceof String ->
                list.stream().map(item -> Enum.valueOf(enumClass, item.toString().toUpperCase())).collect(Collectors.toList());
            case Enum<?> enumValue when enumClass.isInstance(enumValue) -> List.of(enumClass.cast(enumValue));
            case String stringValue -> List.of(Enum.valueOf(enumClass, stringValue.toUpperCase()));
            default -> throw new IllegalArgumentException("Field requires a " + enumClass.getSimpleName() + " or List<" + enumClass.getSimpleName() + "> value");
        };
    }

    public static <T extends Enum<T>> T fromClassName(final Object o, final Class<T> enumType) {
        String name = NORMALIZE.matcher(o.getClass().getSimpleName()).replaceAll("$1_$2").toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
        return Enums.getForNameIgnoreCase(name, enumType);
    }

    private Enums() {
    }
}

   124	        if (elements.length > 0) {

    private List<QueryFilter> formatScopeFilters(QueryFilter filter) {
        String systemNamespace = kestraConfig.getSystemFlowNamespace();
        List<String> scopes = switch (filter.value()) {
            case List<?> list -> list.stream().map(Object::toString).toList();
            case String value -> Arrays.stream(value.split(",")).map(String::trim).filter(scope -> !scope.isEmpty()).toList();
            case Object value -> List.of(value.toString());
        };

        boolean user = scopes.stream().anyMatch(scope -> "USER".equalsIgnoreCase(scope));
        boolean system = scopes.stream().anyMatch(scope -> "SYSTEM".equalsIgnoreCase(scope));

        return switch (filter.operation()) {
            case EQUALS, IN -> user
                ? system ? Collections.emptyList() : List.of(QueryFilter.builder().field(QueryFilter.Field.NAMESPACE).operation(QueryFilter.Op.NOT_EQUALS).value(systemNamespace).build())
                : system ? List.of(QueryFilter.builder().field(QueryFilter.Field.NAMESPACE).operation(QueryFilter.Op.EQUALS).value(systemNamespace).build()) : Collections.emptyList();
            case NOT_EQUALS, NOT_IN -> user
                ? system ? List.of(QueryFilter.builder().field(QueryFilter.Field.NAMESPACE).operation(QueryFilter.Op.EQUALS).value("__scope_never_matches__").build())
                : List.of(QueryFilter.builder().field(QueryFilter.Field.NAMESPACE).operation(QueryFilter.Op.EQUALS).value(systemNamespace).build())
                : system ? List.of(QueryFilter.builder().field(QueryFilter.Field.NAMESPACE).operation(QueryFilter.Op.NOT_EQUALS).value(systemNamespace).build()) : Collections.emptyList();
            default -> List.of(filter);
        };
    }'

+set -euo pipefail
+cd /testbed
+python3 - <<'PY'
+from pathlib import Path
+q = Path('core/src/main/java/io/kestra/core/models/QueryFilter.java').read_text()
+if 'SCOPE("scope") {\n            @Override\n            public List<Op> supportedOp() {\n                return List.of(Op.EQUALS, Op.NOT_EQUALS, Op.IN, Op.NOT_IN);\n            }\n        }' not in q:

+ui = Path('ui/src/components/filter/configurations/dashboardFilters.ts').read_text()
+if 'key: "scope"' not in ui:
+    raise SystemExit('FAIL: dashboard filter configuration does not expose scope filter')
+for token in ['Comparators.EQUALS', 'Comparators.NOT_EQUALS', 'Comparators.IN', 'Comparators.NOT_IN']:
+    if token not in ui:
+        raise SystemExit(f'FAIL: missing {token} in dashboard filter configuration')
+ctrl = Path('webserver/src/main/java/io/kestra/webserver/controllers/api/DashboardController.java').read_text()
+if 'formatScopeFilters' not in ctrl:
+    raise SystemExit('FAIL: dashboard backend does not translate scope filters')
+print('PASS')
+PY

+    private List<QueryFilter> formatScopeFilters(QueryFilter filter) {
+        String systemNamespace = kestraConfig.getSystemFlowNamespace();
+        List<String> scopes = switch (filter.value()) {
+            case List<?> list -> list.stream().map(Object::toString).toList();
+            case String value -> Arrays.stream(value.split(",")).map(String::trim).filter(scope -> !scope.isEmpty()).toList();
+            case Object value -> List.of(value.toString());
+        };
+
+        boolean user = scopes.stream().anyMatch(scope -> "USER".equalsIgnoreCase(scope));
+        boolean system = scopes.stream().anyMatch(scope -> "SYSTEM".equalsIgnoreCase(scope));
+
+        return switch (filter.operation()) {
+            case EQUALS, IN -> user
+                ? system ? Collections.emptyList() : List.of(QueryFilter.builder().field(QueryFilter.Field.NAMESPACE).operation(QueryFilter.Op.NOT_EQUALS).value(systemNamespace).build())
+                : system ? List.of(QueryFilter.builder().field(QueryFilter.Field.NAMESPACE).operation(QueryFilter.Op.EQUALS).value(systemNamespace).build()) : Collections.emptyList();
+            case NOT_EQUALS, NOT_IN -> user
+                ? system ? List.of(
+                    QueryFilter.builder().field(QueryFilter.Field.NAMESPACE).operation(QueryFilter.Op.EQUALS).value(systemNamespace).build(),
+                    QueryFilter.builder().field(QueryFilter.Field.NAMESPACE).operation(QueryFilter.Op.NOT_EQUALS).value(systemNamespace).build()
+                )
+                : List.of(QueryFilter.builder().field(QueryFilter.Field.NAMESPACE).operation(QueryFilter.Op.EQUALS).value(systemNamespace).build())
+                : system ? List.of(QueryFilter.builder().field(QueryFilter.Field.NAMESPACE).operation(QueryFilter.Op.NOT_EQUALS).value(systemNamespace).build()) : Collections.emptyList();
+            default -> List.of(filter);
+        };
+    }
